84|9fce4f|struct FuzzyMatcher {
85|ae76bd|    static func score(query: String, target: String) -> Int? {
86|34cef6|        guard !query.isEmpty else { return 1000 }
87|d6ed84|        
88|aa4292|        let queryLower = query.lowercased()
89|18ea38|        let targetLower = target.lowercased()
90|d6ed84|        
91|c33784|        // Exact match gets highest score
92|bea5c7|        if targetLower == queryLower { return 10000 }
93|d6ed84|        
94|bffced|        // Contains full query
95|8cd767|        if targetLower.contains(queryLower) {
96|1063f5|            // Bonus for starting with query
97|d0876a|            if targetLower.hasPrefix(queryLower) {
98|2e989d|                return 5000 + (1000 - target.count)
99|a7dc16|            }
100|c9ab09|            return 3000 + (1000 - target.count)
101|5f3077|        }
102|d6ed84|        
103|83786c|        // Fuzzy character matching
104|65f313|        var queryIndex = queryLower.startIndex
105|7f11d4|        var targetIndex = targetLower.startIndex
106|268b95|        var score = 0
107|5dc28e|        var consecutiveBonus = 0
108|1d718f|        var lastMatchIndex: String.Index? = nil
109|d6ed84|        
110|308cfe|        while queryIndex < queryLower.endIndex && targetIndex < targetLower.endIndex {
111|c13bec|            if queryLower[queryIndex] == targetLower[targetIndex] {
112|145bbf|                score += 100 + consecutiveBonus
113|216278|                
114|d6ef12|                // Bonus for consecutive matches
115|9f661a|                if let lastIdx = lastMatchIndex,
116|83874f|                   targetLower.index(after: lastIdx) == targetIndex {
117|9c7108|                    consecutiveBonus += 50
118|fdd0e2|                } else {
119|51d442|                    consecutiveBonus = 0
120|4e2d32|                }
121|216278|                
122|c7d2d9|                // Bonus for matching at word boundaries
123|3c44b0|                if targetIndex == targetLower.startIndex ||
124|75c499|                   !targetLower[targetLower.index(before: targetIndex)].isLetter {
125|78d351|                    score += 75
126|4e2d32|                }
127|216278|                
128|b7133b|                lastMatchIndex = targetIndex
129|ea161d|                queryIndex = queryLower.index(after: queryIndex)
130|a7dc16|            }
131|916731|            targetIndex = targetLower.index(after: targetIndex)
132|5f3077|        }
133|d6ed84|        
134|989e1f|        // All query characters must be found
135|0160b5|        guard queryIndex == queryLower.endIndex else { return nil }
136|d6ed84|        
137|c07521|        return score
138|27e597|    }
139|b4687f|    
140|ace7c9|    static func highlight(query: String, in text: String) -> [(String, Bool)] {
141|81813c|        guard !query.isEmpty else { return [(text, false)] }
142|d6ed84|        
143|b880d0|        var result: [(String, Bool)] = []
144|aa4292|        let queryLower = query.lowercased()
145|a14f23|        let textLower = text.lowercased()
146|d6ed84|        
147|65f313|        var queryIndex = queryLower.startIndex
148|a07ffc|        var currentSegment = ""
149|d3c359|        var isMatch = false
150|d6ed84|        
151|4083e9|        for (i, char) in text.enumerated() {
152|212094|            let textIndex = textLower.index(textLower.startIndex, offsetBy: i)
153|3070d1|            
154|3f747d|            if queryIndex < queryLower.endIndex && 
155|f8248a|               textLower[textIndex] == queryLower[queryIndex] {
156|eecabe|                if !isMatch && !currentSegment.isEmpty {
157|78ec19|                    result.append((currentSegment, false))
158|cc1904|                    currentSegment = ""
159|4e2d32|                }
160|a00101|                isMatch = true
161|b31654|                currentSegment.append(char)
162|ea161d|                queryIndex = queryLower.index(after: queryIndex)
163|f5a6eb|            } else {
164|fbac5d|                if isMatch && !currentSegment.isEmpty {
165|15ba04|                    result.append((currentSegment, true))
166|cc1904|                    currentSegment = ""
167|4e2d32|                }
168|d1cc2f|                isMatch = false
169|b31654|                currentSegment.append(char)
170|a7dc16|            }
171|5f3077|        }
172|d6ed84|        
173|5d8d48|        if !currentSegment.isEmpty {
174|eb146d|            result.append((currentSegment, isMatch))
175|5f3077|        }
176|d6ed84|        
177|67ed82|        return result
178|27e597|    }

82|af0ecd|// MARK: - Fuzzy Search
83|adc83b|
84|9fce4f|struct FuzzyMatcher {
85|ae76bd|    static func score(query: String, target: String) -> Int? {
86|34cef6|        guard !query.isEmpty else { return 1000 }
87|d6ed84|        
88|aa4292|        let queryLower = query.lowercased()
89|18ea38|        let targetLower = target.lowercased()
90|d6ed84|        
91|c33784|        // Exact match gets highest score
92|bea5c7|        if targetLower == queryLower { return 10000 }
93|d6ed84|        
94|bffced|        // Contains full query
95|8cd767|        if targetLower.contains(queryLower) {
96|1063f5|            // Bonus for starting with query
97|d0876a|            if targetLower.hasPrefix(queryLower) {
98|2e989d|                return 5000 + (1000 - target.count)
99|a7dc16|            }
100|c9ab09|            return 3000 + (1000 - target.count)
101|5f3077|        }
102|d6ed84|        
103|83786c|        // Fuzzy character matching
104|65f313|        var queryIndex = queryLower.startIndex
105|7f11d4|        var targetIndex = targetLower.startIndex
106|268b95|        var score = 0
107|5dc28e|        var consecutiveBonus = 0
108|1d718f|        var lastMatchIndex: String.Index? = nil
109|d6ed84|        
110|308cfe|        while queryIndex < queryLower.endIndex && targetIndex < targetLower.endIndex {
111|c13bec|            if queryLower[queryIndex] == targetLower[targetIndex] {
112|145bbf|                score += 100 + consecutiveBonus
113|216278|                
114|d6ef12|                // Bonus for consecutive matches
115|9f661a|                if let lastIdx = lastMatchIndex,
116|83874f|                   targetLower.index(after: lastIdx) == targetIndex {
117|9c7108|                    consecutiveBonus += 50
118|fdd0e2|                } else {
119|51d442|                    consecutiveBonus = 0
120|4e2d32|                }
121|216278|                
122|c7d2d9|                // Bonus for matching at word boundaries
123|3c44b0|                if targetIndex == targetLower.startIndex ||
124|75c499|                   !targetLower[targetLower.index(before: targetIndex)].isLetter {
125|78d351|                    score += 75
126|4e2d32|                }
127|216278|                
128|b7133b|                lastMatchIndex = targetIndex
129|ea161d|                queryIndex = queryLower.index(after: queryIndex)
130|a7dc16|            }
131|916731|            targetIndex = targetLower.index(after: targetIndex)
132|5f3077|        }
133|d6ed84|        
134|989e1f|        // All query characters must be found
135|0160b5|        guard queryIndex == queryLower.endIndex else { return nil }
136|d6ed84|        
137|c07521|        return score
138|27e597|    }
139|b4687f|    
140|ace7c9|    static func highlight(query: String, in text: String) -> [(String, Bool)] {
141|81813c|        guard !query.isEmpty else { return [(text, false)] }
142|d6ed84|        
143|b880d0|        var result: [(String, Bool)] = []
144|aa4292|        let queryLower = query.lowercased()
145|a14f23|        let textLower = text.lowercased()
146|d6ed84|        
147|65f313|        var queryIndex = queryLower.startIndex
148|a07ffc|        var currentSegment = ""
149|d3c359|        var isMatch = false
150|d6ed84|        
151|4083e9|        for (i, char) in text.enumerated() {
152|212094|            let textIndex = textLower.index(textLower.startIndex, offsetBy: i)
153|3070d1|            
154|3f747d|            if queryIndex < queryLower.endIndex && 
155|f8248a|               textLower[textIndex] == queryLower[queryIndex] {
156|eecabe|                if !isMatch && !currentSegment.isEmpty {
157|78ec19|                    result.append((currentSegment, false))
158|cc1904|                    currentSegment = ""
159|4e2d32|                }
160|a00101|                isMatch = true
161|b31654|                currentSegment.append(char)
162|ea161d|                queryIndex = queryLower.index(after: queryIndex)
163|f5a6eb|            } else {
164|fbac5d|                if isMatch && !currentSegment.isEmpty {
165|15ba04|                    result.append((currentSegment, true))
166|cc1904|                    currentSegment = ""
167|4e2d32|                }
168|d1cc2f|                isMatch = false
169|b31654|                currentSegment.append(char)
170|a7dc16|            }
171|5f3077|        }
172|d6ed84|        
173|5d8d48|        if !currentSegment.isEmpty {
174|eb146d|            result.append((currentSegment, isMatch))
175|5f3077|        }
176|d6ed84|        
177|67ed82|        return result
178|27e597|    }

404|b4687f|    
405|27623f|    private var filteredCommands: [Command] {
406|93055c|        if searchText.isEmpty {
407|c6a1fd|            // Show recent commands first, then all commands
408|df481a|            let recentNames = Set(recentManager.recentCommands)
409|28414c|            let recent = allCommands.filter { recentNames.contains($0.name) }
410|af65a0|                .sorted { a, b in
411|d73b49|                    let aIdx = recentManager.recentCommands.firstIndex(of: a.name) ?? Int.max
412|3d02c9|                    let bIdx = recentManager.recentCommands.firstIndex(of: b.name) ?? Int.max
413|0688f6|                    return aIdx < bIdx
414|4e2d32|                }
415|c4a108|            let others = allCommands.filter { !recentNames.contains($0.name) }
416|4f9548|            return recent + others
417|5f3077|        }
418|d6ed84|        
419|babd96|        return allCommands
420|519b5d|            .compactMap { cmd -> (Command, Int)? in
421|8c516a|                guard let score = FuzzyMatcher.score(query: searchText, target: cmd.name) else {
422|024b84|                    return nil
423|4e2d32|                }
424|46f56b|                return (cmd, score)
425|a7dc16|            }
426|4a2f11|            .sorted { $0.1 > $1.1 }
427|ffcc79|            .map { $0.0 }
428|27e597|    }
429|b4687f|    
430|debdc2|    private func dismiss() {
431|02562c|        editorCore.showCommandPalette = false
432|27e597|    }
433|b4687f|    
434|3b5568|    private func executeCommand(_ command: Command) {
435|0a37ea|        recentManager.addRecent(command.name)
436|a6f1ca|        command.action()
437|27e597|    }

617|4c9b69|        if searchQuery.isEmpty {

import SwiftUI

/// Reusable git branch selector + management menu.
struct BranchMenu<Label: View>: View {
    @ObservedObject var git: GitManager
    let label: () -> Label
    
    @State private var showCreateBranchAlert: Bool = false
    @State private var newBranchName: String = ""
    @State private var pendingDeleteBranch: String? = nil
    @State private var showErrorAlert: Bool = false
    @State private var errorMessage: String = ""
    @State private var showDeleteAlert: Bool = false
    
    private var localBranches: [GitBranch] {
        git.branches.filter { !$0.isRemote }
    }
    
    private var deletableBranches: [GitBranch] {
        localBranches.filter { !$0.isCurrent }
    }
    
    var body: some View {
        Menu {
            branchListSection
            Divider()
            createBranchButton
            deleteBranchMenu
        } label: {
            label()

//
//  CommandPalette.swift
//  VSCodeiPadOS
//
//  VS Code-style Command Palette with fuzzy search
//

import SwiftUI

// MARK: - Command Definition

struct Command: Identifiable, Equatable {
    let id = UUID()
    let name: String
    let shortcut: String?
    let icon: String
    let category: CommandCategory
    let action: () -> Void
    
    static func == (lhs: Command, rhs: Command) -> Bool {
        lhs.id == rhs.id
    }
}

enum CommandCategory: String, CaseIterable {
    case file = "File"
    case edit = "Edit"
    case selection = "Selection"
    case view = "View"
    case go = "Go"

=== VSCodeiPadOS/VSCodeiPadOS/Views/CommandPaletteView.swift ===
import SwiftUI

struct CommandPaletteView: View {
    @Environment(\.dismiss) private var dismiss
    @ObservedObject var editorCore: EditorCore
    @State private var searchText = ""
    @State private var commandCategories: [CommandCategory] = []
    
    var filteredCommands: [CommandCategory] {
        if searchText.isEmpty {
            return commandCategories
        }
        return commandCategories.map { category in
            CommandCategory(
                name: category.name,
                commands: category.commands.filter { command in
                    command.title.localizedCaseInsensitiveContains(searchText) ||
                    command.keywords.contains { $0.localizedCaseInsensitiveContains(searchText) }
                }
            )
        }.filter { !$0.commands.isEmpty }
    }
    
    var body: some View {
        NavigationView {
            List {
                ForEach(filteredCommands, id: \.name) { category in
                    Section(header: Text(category.name)) {
                        ForEach(category.commands, id: \.title) { command in
                            Button(action: {

    let isOpen: Bool

            ("Command Palette", "p", [.command, .shift], #selector(cmdPalette)),
            ("AI Assistant", "a", [.command, .shift], #selector(cmdAIAssistant)),
            ("Toggle Terminal", "j", [.command], #selector(cmdToggleTerminal)),
            ("Toggle Sidebar", "b", [.command], #selector(cmdToggleSidebar)),
            ("Quick Open", "p", [.command], #selector(cmdQuickOpen)),
            ("New File", "n", [.command], #selector(cmdNewFile)),
            ("Save", "s", [.command], #selector(cmdSave)),
            ("Close Tab", "w", [.command], #selector(cmdCloseTab)),
            ("Find", "f", [.command], #selector(cmdFind)),
            ("Go to Line", "g", [.control], #selector(cmdGoToLine)),
            ("Zoom In", "=", [.command], #selector(cmdZoomIn)),
            ("Zoom Out", "-", [.command], #selector(cmdZoomOut)),
        ]
        return defs.map { (title, input, mods, action) in
            let cmd = UIKeyCommand(title: title, action: action, input: input, modifierFlags: mods)
            cmd.wantsPriorityOverSystemBehavior = true
            return cmd
        }
    }

        self.name = name

=== VSCodeiPadOS/VSCodeiPadOS/Views/SnippetPickerView.swift ===
import SwiftUI

struct SnippetPickerView: View {
    @ObservedObject var editorCore: EditorCore
    @ObservedObject private var snippetsManager = SnippetsManager.shared

    @State private var searchText = ""
    @State private var selectedIndex = 0
    @FocusState private var isSearchFocused: Bool

    private var language: CodeLanguage? {
        editorCore.activeTab?.language
    }

    private var allSnippets: [Snippet] {
        snippetsManager.allSnippets(language: language)
    }

    private var filteredSnippets: [Snippet] {
        guard !searchText.isEmpty else { return allSnippets }

        return allSnippets
            .compactMap { snip -> (Snippet, Int)? in
                let haystack = "\(snip.name) \(snip.prefix) \(snip.description)"
                guard let score = FuzzyMatcher.score(query: searchText, target: haystack) else {
                    return nil
                }
                return (snip, score)
            }
            .sorted { $0.1 > $1.1 }

import SwiftUI

struct BreadcrumbsView: View {
    @ObservedObject var editorCore: EditorCore
    let tab: Tab
    
    var pathComponents: [String] {
        if let url = tab.url {
            // Use standard components
            return url.pathComponents.filter { $0 != "/" }
        }
        return ["VSCodeiPadOS", "Views", tab.fileName]
    }
    
    var body: some View {
        ScrollView(.horizontal, showsIndicators: false) {
            HStack(spacing: 2) {
                ForEach(Array(pathComponents.enumerated()), id: \.offset) { index, component in
                    let isLast = index == pathComponents.count - 1
                    
                    // Breadcrumb item
                    HStack(spacing: 4) {
                        if index == 0 {
                            Image(systemName: "folder")
                                .font(.caption2)

import SwiftUI

struct EditorSplitView: View {
    @ObservedObject var editorCore: EditorCore
    let tab: Tab
    let theme: Theme
    @State private var showPreview = false
    
    private var isMarkdown: Bool {
        tab.fileName.lowercased().hasSuffix(".md")
    }

    var body: some View {
        HStack(spacing: 0) {
            IDEEditorView(editorCore: editorCore, tab: tab, theme: theme)
                .frame(maxWidth: showPreview ? UIScreen.main.bounds.width * 0.5 : .infinity)
            
            if showPreview && isMarkdown {
                Rectangle()
                    .fill(Color.gray.opacity(0.3))
                    .frame(width: 1)
                
                MarkdownPreviewWrapper(editorCore: editorCore, tab: tab)
                    .frame(maxWidth: .infinity)
            }

=== VSCodeiPadOS/VSCodeiPadOS/Views/Editor/FoldingLayoutManager.swift ===
import UIKit

/// TextKit layout manager that collapses line fragments for lines marked folded in CodeFoldingManager.
/// This is a view-level folding implementation (it does NOT modify the underlying text).

final class FoldingLayoutManager: NSLayoutManager, NSLayoutManagerDelegate {
    weak var ownerTextView: EditorTextView?
    private var foldingObserver: NSObjectProtocol?

    override init() {
        super.init()
        self.delegate = self
        setupFoldingObserver()
    }

    required init?(coder: NSCoder) {
        super.init(coder: coder)
        self.delegate = self
        setupFoldingObserver()
    }

    deinit {
        if let observer = foldingObserver {
            NotificationCenter.default.removeObserver(observer)
        }

import SwiftUI

/// VS Code–style minimap with:
/// - syntax-colored tiny preview
/// - visible region overlay
/// - tap/drag to scroll
/// - optional git diff indicators (added/modified/deleted)
struct MinimapView: View {
    // MARK: - External inputs

    let content: String
    /// Current scroll offset (read-only for display). Minimap FOLLOWS the editor, never fights it.
    let scrollOffset: CGFloat
    /// Visible viewport height (read-only for display)
    let scrollViewHeight: CGFloat
    let totalContentHeight: CGFloat
    
    /// Callback when user taps/drags on minimap to request scroll. 
    /// Parent handles actual scrolling - prevents bidirectional binding jitter.
    var onScrollRequested: ((CGFloat) -> Void)? = nil

    /// Optional indicators to render as thin bars on the left side of the minimap.
    /// Note: call sites can ignore this (default empty) without breaking compilation.
    var diffIndicators: [MinimapDiffIndicator] = []


=== VSCodeiPadOS/VSCodeiPadOS/Views/Editor/ModifierTapGestureRecognizer.swift ===
import UIKit

/// UITapGestureRecognizer that captures the modifier flags (Option/Shift/Cmd/etc) active at the time of the tap.
///
/// UIKit doesn't expose the UIEvent in the selector callback, so we store it from touchesBegan.
final class ModifierTapGestureRecognizer: UITapGestureRecognizer {
    private(set) var lastModifierFlags: UIEvent.ModifierFlags = []

    override func touchesBegan(_ touches: Set<UITouch>, with event: UIEvent) {
        lastModifierFlags = event.modifierFlags
        super.touchesBegan(touches, with: event)
    }

    override func touchesMoved(_ touches: Set<UITouch>, with event: UIEvent) {
        lastModifierFlags = event.modifierFlags
        super.touchesMoved(touches, with: event)
    }
}

=== VSCodeiPadOS/VSCodeiPadOS/Views/Editor/StickyHeaderView.swift ===
import SwiftUI

struct StickyHeaderView: View {
    let text: String
    let currentLine: Int
    let theme: Theme
    let lineHeight: CGFloat
    let onSelect: (Int) -> Void
    
    @State private var stickyLines: [(line: Int, content: String, depth: Int)] = []
    
    var body: some View {
        VStack(alignment: .leading, spacing: 0) {
            ForEach(stickyLines, id: \.line) { item in
                HStack {
                    Text(item.content.trimmingCharacters(in: .whitespaces))
                        .font(.system(size: 14, weight: .regular, design: .monospaced))
                        .foregroundColor(theme.editorForeground)
                        .padding(.leading, CGFloat(item.depth) * 16 + 4)
                        .padding(.vertical, 2)
                    Spacer()
                }
                .frame(height: lineHeight)
                .background(theme.editorBackground.opacity(0.95))
                .overlay(Rectangle().frame(height: 1).foregroundColor(theme.sidebarBackground), alignment: .bottom)

82|af0ecd|// MARK: - Fuzzy Search
83|adc83b|
84|9fce4f|struct FuzzyMatcher {
85|ae76bd|    static func score(query: String, target: String) -> Int? {
86|34cef6|        guard !query.isEmpty else { return 1000 }
87|d6ed84|        
88|aa4292|        let queryLower = query.lowercased()
89|18ea38|        let targetLower = target.lowercased()
90|d6ed84|        
91|c33784|        // Exact match gets highest score
92|bea5c7|        if targetLower == queryLower { return 10000 }
93|d6ed84|        
94|bffced|        // Contains full query
95|8cd767|        if targetLower.contains(queryLower) {
96|1063f5|            // Bonus for starting with query
97|d0876a|            if targetLower.hasPrefix(queryLower) {
98|2e989d|                return 5000 + (1000 - target.count)
99|a7dc16|            }
100|c9ab09|            return 3000 + (1000 - target.count)
101|5f3077|        }
102|d6ed84|        
103|83786c|        // Fuzzy character matching
104|65f313|        var queryIndex = queryLower.startIndex
105|7f11d4|        var targetIndex = targetLower.startIndex
106|268b95|        var score = 0
107|5dc28e|        var consecutiveBonus = 0
108|1d718f|        var lastMatchIndex: String.Index? = nil
109|d6ed84|        
110|308cfe|        while queryIndex < queryLower.endIndex && targetIndex < targetLower.endIndex {
111|c13bec|            if queryLower[queryIndex] == targetLower[targetIndex] {
112|145bbf|                score += 100 + consecutiveBonus
113|216278|                
114|d6ef12|                // Bonus for consecutive matches
115|9f661a|                if let lastIdx = lastMatchIndex,
116|83874f|                   targetLower.index(after: lastIdx) == targetIndex {
117|9c7108|                    consecutiveBonus += 50
118|fdd0e2|                } else {
119|51d442|                    consecutiveBonus = 0
120|4e2d32|                }
121|216278|                
122|c7d2d9|                // Bonus for matching at word boundaries
123|3c44b0|                if targetIndex == targetLower.startIndex ||
124|75c499|                   !targetLower[targetLower.index(before: targetIndex)].isLetter {
125|78d351|                    score += 75
126|4e2d32|                }
127|216278|                
128|b7133b|                lastMatchIndex = targetIndex
129|ea161d|                queryIndex = queryLower.index(after: queryIndex)
130|a7dc16|            }
131|916731|            targetIndex = targetLower.index(after: targetIndex)
132|5f3077|        }
133|d6ed84|        
134|989e1f|        // All query characters must be found
135|0160b5|        guard queryIndex == queryLower.endIndex else { return nil }
136|d6ed84|        
137|c07521|        return score
138|27e597|    }
139|b4687f|    
140|ace7c9|    static func highlight(query: String, in text: String) -> [(String, Bool)] {
141|81813c|        guard !query.isEmpty else { return [(text, false)] }
142|d6ed84|        
143|b880d0|        var result: [(String, Bool)] = []
144|aa4292|        let queryLower = query.lowercased()
145|a14f23|        let textLower = text.lowercased()
146|d6ed84|        
147|65f313|        var queryIndex = queryLower.startIndex
148|a07ffc|        var currentSegment = ""
149|d3c359|        var isMatch = false
150|d6ed84|        
151|4083e9|        for (i, char) in text.enumerated() {
152|212094|            let textIndex = textLower.index(textLower.startIndex, offsetBy: i)
153|3070d1|            
154|3f747d|            if queryIndex < queryLower.endIndex && 
155|f8248a|               textLower[textIndex] == queryLower[queryIndex] {
156|eecabe|                if !isMatch && !currentSegment.isEmpty {
157|78ec19|                    result.append((currentSegment, false))
158|cc1904|                    currentSegment = ""
159|4e2d32|                }
160|a00101|                isMatch = true
161|b31654|                currentSegment.append(char)
162|ea161d|                queryIndex = queryLower.index(after: queryIndex)
163|f5a6eb|            } else {
164|fbac5d|                if isMatch && !currentSegment.isEmpty {
165|15ba04|                    result.append((currentSegment, true))
166|cc1904|                    currentSegment = ""
167|4e2d32|                }
168|d1cc2f|                isMatch = false
169|b31654|                currentSegment.append(char)
170|a7dc16|            }
171|5f3077|        }
172|d6ed84|        
173|5d8d48|        if !currentSegment.isEmpty {
174|eb146d|            result.append((currentSegment, isMatch))
175|5f3077|        }
176|d6ed84|        
177|67ed82|        return result
178|27e597|    }

130|2b113b|    func updateUIView(_ textView: TextView, context: Context) {

132|aa6fd6|        context.coordinator.parent = self

137|0ae3b4|            context.coordinator.lastThemeId = currentThemeId

140|5f3077|        }
141|d6ed84|

151|ed0ffc|            textView.isLineWrappingEnabled = wordWrapEnabled
152|5f3077|        }

154|26756b|        // CRITICAL: Only call setState() when safe (not during active editing)

156|092fab|        // and causes crash at TextEditHelper.swift:27 (force unwrap on linePosition)

171|f5a6eb|            } else {
172|8d685d|                textView.text = text
173|a7dc16|            }
174|3070d1|            
175|80f64f|            // CRITICAL: Re-apply theme AFTER setState - setState may reset rendering state
176|cd161e|            textView.theme = makeRunestoneTheme()
177|3070d1|

179|f89f38|            textView.selectedRange = NSRange(location: 0, length: 0)
180|3070d1|

182|ebb427|            DispatchQueue.main.async {

184|a7dc16|            }
185|8bc7f3|        } else if textChanged && !context.coordinator.hasBeenEdited && !isActivelyEditing && !context.coordinator.isUpdatingFromTextView {

187|51a126|            // Safe to update since user hasn't started editing yet

192|8d685d|                textView.text = text
193|a7dc16|            }

197|3070d1|

201|a7dc16|            }
202|5f3077|        }

205|27e597|    }

237|70f3e8|    /// Gets the actual TreeSitter Language object for a given filename
238|f3a5e1|    /// Returns nil for plain text files (no syntax highlighting)
239|a4a35b|    private func getTreeSitterLanguage(for filename: String) -> Runestone.TreeSitterLanguage? {
240|98942b|        let ext = (filename as NSString).pathExtension.lowercased()
241|82335e|        let lastComponent = (filename as NSString).lastPathComponent.lowercased()
242|d6ed84|

244|013551|        if lastComponent == "dockerfile" || lastComponent.hasPrefix("dockerfile.") {

123|ab06c2|    @ViewBuilder
124|e053f1|    private func diffIndicatorsLayer(minimapHeight: CGFloat, lineCount: Int) -> some View {
125|df88d3|        // VS Code minimap diff markers are thin and pinned to the left.
126|352402|        let barWidth: CGFloat = 2
127|adc83b|
128|eb7497|        // Guard against division by zero
129|dad1b1|        if lineCount > 0 {
130|82ebe9|            ForEach(diffIndicators) { indicator in
131|c4c9a2|                let startLine = max(0, min(indicator.lineRange.lowerBound, lineCount - 1))
132|d34bb2|                let endLineExclusive = max(startLine + 1, min(indicator.lineRange.upperBound, lineCount))
133|adc83b|
134|7e47a5|                let startY = (CGFloat(startLine) / CGFloat(max(lineCount, 1))) * minimapHeight
135|634593|                let endY = (CGFloat(endLineExclusive) / CGFloat(max(lineCount, 1))) * minimapHeight
136|13ec78|                let height = max(2, endY - startY)
137|adc83b|
138|ff13e9|                Rectangle()
139|41dcad|                    .fill(diffColor(for: indicator.kind).opacity(0.95))
140|81c659|                    .frame(width: barWidth, height: height)
141|72358e|                    .offset(x: 0, y: startY)
142|a7dc16|            }
143|5f3077|        }
144|27e597|    }

146|906d12|    // MARK: - Visible region math
147|adc83b|
148|6919f3|    private func visibleRegionHeight(minimapHeight: CGFloat) -> CGFloat {
149|ff17e8|        guard totalContentHeight > 0 else { return 0 }
150|c5f520|        let ratio = scrollViewHeight / totalContentHeight
151|f9bc55|        return minimapHeight * min(max(ratio, 0), 1.0)
152|27e597|    }
153|adc83b|
154|ee5041|    private func visibleRegionOffset(minimapHeight: CGFloat, visibleHeight: CGFloat) -> CGFloat {
155|7da55c|        let scrollable = max(0, totalContentHeight - scrollViewHeight)

168|dac0ba|        guard let onScrollRequested = onScrollRequested else { return }
169|adc83b|
170|783533|        let clampedY = max(0, min(yPosition, minimapHeight))
171|89fa92|        let ratio = (minimapHeight > 0) ? (clampedY / minimapHeight) : 0
172|adc83b|

182|27e597|    }
